style="margin-top:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">NORWALK, Conn., December&#160;21, 2021 - FactSet (&#34;FactSet&#34; or the &#8220;Company&#8221;) (NYSE&#58;FDS) (NASDAQ&#58;FDS), a global provider of integrated financial information, analytical applications, and industry-leading service, today announced results for its first quarter ended November&#160;30, 2021. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;margin-top:15pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">First Quarter Fiscal 2022 Highlights</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:700;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Revenues</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> increased 9.4%, or $36.5 million, to $424.7 million for the first quarter of fiscal 2022 compared with $388.2 million for the same period in fiscal 2021. The increase was primarily due to higher sales of analytics and research and advisory solutions. Organic revenues, which excludes the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed within the last 12 months and foreign currency movements, grew 9.1% to $423.2 million during the first quarter of fiscal 2022 from the prior year period. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:700;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Annual Subscription Value</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> (ASV) plus professional services was $1.7 billion at November&#160;30, 2021, compared with $1.6 billion at November&#160;30, 2020. </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Organic ASV plus professional services, </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">which excludes the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed within the last 12 months and foreign currency movements,</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> was also $1.7 billion at November&#160;30, 2021, up $142.3 million from the prior year at a growth rate of 8.9%. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:700;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Organic ASV </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">plus professional services increased $16.9 million over the last three months. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">The primary contributors to this growth were higher sales of analytics and research and advisory solutions. Please see the &#8220;ASV + Professional Services&#8221; section of this press release for details.</font></div><div style="padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:132%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:700;line-height:132%;padding-left:14.85pt">GAAP operating margin </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:132%">decreased to 28.9% compared with 31.2% for the same period last year, mainly driven by restructuring costs and real estate exit costs. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:132%">Adjusted operating margin decreased to 33.6% compared with 34.3% in the prior year period, primarily as a result of increased infrastructure expenses and data costs, partially offset by lower compensation expenses.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:700;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Diluted GAAP earnings per share </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">(EPS) increased 6.5% to $2.79 compared with $2.62 for the same period in fiscal 2021. Adjusted diluted EPS increased 12.8% to $3.25 compared with the prior year period, primarily due to higher revenues and a decreased tax rate. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">The Company&#8217;s</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:700;line-height:133%"> effective tax rate</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> for the first quarter decreased to 10.2% compared with 15.8% a year ago, primarily due to higher than expected tax benefit associated with the exercise of stock options in the current quarter compared with the three months ended November&#160;30, 2020. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">FactSet acquired Cobalt Software, Inc., a leading portfolio monitoring solutions provider for the private capital industry, in October 2021.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">FactSet reaffirms its annual outlook for fiscal 2022 as provided in September 2021. Please see the &#8220;Annual Business Outlook&#8221; section of this press release for details.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8220;I&#8217;m pleased to report that FactSet once again delivered impressive quarterly results, reflecting the continuing momentum in our business,&#8221; said Phil Snow, CEO, FactSet. &#8220;It is clear that the investments we have made in our business are paying off in top line growth. Demand for differentiated content remains strong, which we intend to capitalize on with our leading open content and analytics platform.&#8221;</font></div><div release. </font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8220;Underpinning our accelerating margin and a 33.6% operating margin on an adjusted basis, which exceeds our fiscal 2022 adjusted operating margin guidance of 32.5% to 33.5%.&#8221;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;margin-top:15pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Annual Subscription Value (ASV) + Professional Services </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV at any given point in time represents the forward-looking revenues for the next twelve months from all subscription services currently supplied to clients. Professional services is revenue derived from project-based consulting and implementation.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV plus professional services was $1,706 million at November&#160;30, 2021 compared with $1,562 million at </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">November&#160;30, 2020</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">. Organic ASV plus professional services was $1,701 million at November&#160;30, 2021, up $142.3 million from the prior year at a growth rate of 8.9%. Organic ASV, which excludes the effects of acquisitions and dispositions </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">completed within the last 12 months</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> and foreign currency movements, plus professional services, increased $16.9 million over the last three months. </font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Buy-side and sell-side ASV growth rates for the first quarter of fiscal 2022 were 8.5% and 13.2%, respectively. Buy-side clients, who primarily include asset managers, asset owners, wealth managers, hedge funds, corporations, and channel partners, accounted for approximately 83% of organic ASV while the remainder came from sell-side firms that include broker-dealers, banking and advisory, private equity and venture capital firms. Supplementary tables covering organic buy-side and sell-side ASV growth rates may be found on the last page of this press release. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;margin-top:15pt"><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Segment Revenues and ASV</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV from the Americas region was $1,054.9 million compared with ASV in the prior year period of </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">$958.5 million.</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> Organic ASV increased 9.4% to $1,048.2 million. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Americas revenues for the quarter increased to $266.9 million compared with $244.3 million in the first quarter last year. Excluding the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed in the last 12 months, the Americas region organic revenues growth rate was 8.5%. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV from the EMEA region was $452.0 million compared with ASV in the prior year period of $422.0 million. Organic ASV increased 7.2% to $453.4 million. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">EMEA revenues were $115.0 million compared with $105.8 million in the first quarter of fiscal 2021. </font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:right"><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:7pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">2</font></div><div style="padding-right:18pt"><font style="color:#dcdcdc;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:6pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:86.4pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">News Release </font><font style="color:#98ca3c;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">I</font><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> For Immediate Release</font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Excluding the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed in the last 12 months and foreign currency impacts, the EMEA region organic revenues growth rate was 8.8%. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV from the Asia Pacific region was $175.4 million compared with ASV in the prior year period of $156.5 million. Organic ASV increased 13.6% to $176.2 million. Asia Pacific revenues were $42.8 million compared with $38.1 million in the first quarter of fiscal 2021. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Excluding the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed in the last 12 months and foreign currency impacts, the Asia Pacific region organic revenues growth rate was 13.7%. </font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Segment ASV does not include professional services, which totaled $24.0 million at November&#160;30, 2021.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;margin-top:15pt"><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Operational Highlights &#8211; First Quarter Fiscal 2022</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Client count as of November&#160;30, 2021 was 6,759, a net increase of 306 clients in the past three months, primarily driven by an increase in corporate clients. The count includes clients with ASV of $10,000 and more.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">User count increased by 1,229 to 162,161 in the past three months, primarily driven by an increase in research and advisory users.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Annual ASV retention was greater than 95%. When expressed as a percentage of clients, annual retention was 92%. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Expense highlights include a restructuring charge of $9 million to drive organizational realignment. Ongoing savings from this realignment primarily will be used for product reinvestment and key talent retention. In addition, the Company recognized $4 million of expense related to vacating certain office space in New York City. The Company recently polled FactSet employees on optimal work arrangements and, consistent with what the Company has seen in the market, the majority of the Company's employees have indicated that they will work in a hybrid or a remote environment. Accordingly, FactSet is reassessing its real estate footprint to better reflect these new work arrangements.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Employee count was 10,898 as of November&#160;30, 2021, up 2.6% over the last twelve months. Excluding acquisitions made over the last twelve months, headcount grew by 1.8% year over year, primarily driven by increased hiring in the Company's content and technology organizations.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Net cash provided by operating activities decreased to $72.9 million compared with $89.3 million for the first quarter of fiscal 2021, primarily due to the timing of tax payments in the UK and higher year-over-year employee bonus payments. Quarterly free cash flow decreased to $64.3 million compared with $70.9 million a year ago, a decrease of 9.3%, primarily due to the timing of tax payments in the UK, higher year-over-year employee bonus payments and a $9.7 million reduction in capital expenditures related to facilities build-outs completed in fiscal 2021.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font 16, 2021 to holders of record of FactSet&#8217;s common stock at the close of business on November&#160;30, 2021. </font></div><div The Company believes that these adjusted financial measures better reflect the underlying economic performance of FactSet.</font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">The GAAP financial measure, cash flows provided by operating activities, has been reduced by capital expenditures to report non-GAAP free cash flow. if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
